Q1	SELECT supplier.s_suppkey, partsupp.ps_suppkey  FROM supplier FULL OUTER JOIN partsupp ON supplier.s_suppkey = partsupp.ps_suppkey   LIMIT 100
Q2	SELECT partsupp.ps_suppkey, partsupp.ps_supplycost, partsupp.ps_availqty  FROM part LEFT OUTER JOIN partsupp ON partsupp.ps_partkey = part.p_partkey  WHERE part.p_retailprice = '905.00' AND part.p_size = 6 AND partsupp.ps_availqty < 1664   LIMIT 100
Q3	SELECT sum(distinct(supplier.s_nationkey)) AS c_10  FROM supplier GROUP BY supplier.s_suppkey   LIMIT 100
Q4	SELECT partsupp.ps_supplycost  FROM partsupp GROUP BY partsupp.ps_supplycost   LIMIT 100
Q5	SELECT orders.o_shippriority, orders.o_custkey  FROM orders  WHERE orders.o_shippriority >= 0 AND orders.o_custkey > 472129 AND orders.o_totalprice = '122444.33' GROUP BY orders.o_custkey, orders.o_shippriority   LIMIT 100
Q6	SELECT variance(partsupp.ps_suppkey) AS c_10  FROM partsupp GROUP BY partsupp.ps_partkey   LIMIT 100
Q7	SELECT orders.o_totalprice, orders.o_orderkey, orders.o_custkey  FROM orders ORDER BY orders.o_custkey ASC   LIMIT 100
Q8	SELECT max(distinct(part.p_retailprice)) AS c_10  FROM part  WHERE part.p_size = 20 AND part.p_retailprice = '905.00' AND part.p_partkey >= 825043 GROUP BY part.p_size, part.p_partkey   LIMIT 100
